1a1(1): bcom ldan 'das bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gsang ba ye shes kyi snying po thams cad yongs su rdzogs
1a2(1): shing 'dus pa dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud chen po zhes bya ba bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du/ b+ha ga wAn+ta ga ta sarba kA ya wA k+Shit+ta/ g+hA ya gnya' na gar+b+ha sarba pa ri pA ri tA sa mA dza shrI g+hA ya sa mu dA ya ma hA tan+ta nA ma/ bod skad du/ bcom ldan 'das bde
1b2(1): pabar gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gsang ba ye shes kyi snying po thams cad yongs su rdzogs shing 'dus pa/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud chen po zhes bya ba/ thams
1b3(1): cad ston pa bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ 'og min chos kyi dbyings kyi pho brang sku gsung thugs rdo rje
1b4(1): rnam dag gsang ba yongs su rdzogs pa mchog gi gnas/ rgya chad phyogs lhung tshad las 'das pa/ rang byung 'od kyi gzhal yas khang na/ ston pa bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu
2a1(1): bzang po/ drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid/ ma bcos spros med byang chub chen po'i ngang nas rang shar nas/ kun bzang yum gyi b+ha ga la snyoms par zhugs te/ kun
2a2(1): gzhi ye nas dag pa'i yum gyi mkha' las/ skye ba'i cho 'phrul du/ e yaM ra suM kai raM b+h+yAM du shar bas e las kun rtog go 'byed nam mkha' mthing nag tu gsal/ yaM las 'jig rten
2a3(1): 'degs byed rlung gi dkyil 'khor ljang gur gsal/ ra las kun skyed rak+ta'i rgya mtsho dmar nag tu gsal/ de las 'dod khams gnas ris nyi shu yongs su rdzogs/ suM las brtan
2a4(1): gzhi gser gyi sa rngams ser nag tu gsal/ de las gzugs khams gnas ris bcu bdun yongs su rdzogs par shar/ raM las 'byung ba drod bsnams bskal pa'i me ri dmar
2b1(1): ser du gsal/ kaM las rten byed rus pa'i ri rab dkar por gsal// de las gzugs med skye mched mu bzhi yongs su rdzogs par shar/ de ltar 'byung ba lnga brtsegs pa'i steng du/ b+h+rUM las ye shes lnga ldan b+han+da
2b2(1): gsar rnying gnam lcags gzer chen 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang kun tu gru bzhi sgo khyud can gcig gi dbus su/ dpal gyi pho brang dgu yongs su rdzogs pa/ dur khrod 'bar ba'i klong / de la lha brgyad kyi ka ba
2b3(1): tshangs pa'i gdung dang bcas pa// klu brgyad kyi ka gdan rgyu skar gyi dral grab can/ nang sgo zang thal ye shes kyi sgo bzhi dang ldan pa ka ba bzhis bdud bzhi bcom pa/ zhi lpags kyi thog/ zhing chen rlon pa'i 'phan
2b4(1): gdugs 'phyar ba/ rgyu ma'i lnga ldi tsit+ta'i pho lto/ thod pa'i dra ba/ rat+na'i pha gu seg na'i dra phyed brgyan pa/ mAM sa'i ri phung / rak+ta'i rdzing bu/ rus pa'i gram pa dang ldan pa/ thod pa'i rta babs dang / chos kyi 'khor
2b5(1): lo chu srin gyis brgyan pa// sgo yang sbrul gyi skyes bu/ chu srin gyi ya zem/ rus sbal gyi ma them/ zhing chen gyi sgo logs byas pa/ sgo khang rgyan dgus spras pa/ rdo rje'i ra ba me ri dmar nag gis bskor ba/ theg pa
2b6(1): mtha' dag yongs su rdzogs pa/ rdo rje'i brag chen la pad+ma dmar po stong ldan du brdal te/ rtsibs stong 'khor lo'i gur phub pa ni rnal 'byor gsum gyi theg mchog yongs su rdzogs pa/ pho brang dbus kyi gdan
3a1(1): yang / ma chags pad+ma'i gdan steng / thabs shes rab nyi zla'i khar/ lha brgyad klu brgyad kyi chings su bsnol ba'i gdan stengs su/ mi 'jigs seng ge dang / dpa' brtul stag dang / rngam pa gzig
3a2(1): dang / gtum pa dom dang / stobs ldan glang po che dang / brjid pa ma he dang / 'jigs pa chu srin dang / zhe sdang sbrul dang / byol song chen po brgyad kyi khri stengs su/ 'khor ba rgyun gcod gser gyi 'khor lo
3a3(1): rtsibs bcu gnyis pa'i stengs su/ chos kyi sku las longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku dpal che mchog he ru ka zhes bya ba/ dus gsum rgyal ba'i sa nyi shu rtsa gcig yongs su rdzogs pa'i brdar/ dbu nyi shu rtsa gcig tu
3a4(1): bstan pa/ chags pa can gyi 'gro ba 'dul ba'i phyir phyag bzhi bcu zhe gnyis na/ zhi ba'i lha bzhi bcu zhe gnyis yab yum thabs dang shes rab kyi tshul du bsnams pa/ zhe sdang can gyi 'gro ba 'dul ba'i phyir/
3a5(1): dpal gyi chas bcus sku la spras pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rje btsan du gyur pa/ gar dgu'i tshul du bzhugs pa/ yum khro mo gnam zhal ma/ dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad ni/ theg pa dgu dang stong pa bco
3a6(1): brgyad yongs su rdzogs tshul du bzhugs pa/ g.yas pa gtso bo la 'khyud pa/ g.yon dung dmar gtso la stob pa/ thabs shes rab yongs su rdzogs brdar/ yab yum gnyis med du sbyor zhing / gzhal yas khang
3b1(1): gdan dang bcas pa la/ 'khor 'das kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i ngang las yab yum sbyor ba mdzad pa'i byang chub sems kyi sprin las/ sbrul sku'i khro bo 'chol pa phyogs bcur 'phros/ lha chen po la
3b2(1): sogs dregs pa can thams cad btul tshar bcad de/ phyogs mtshams brgyad du bting ba las/ sprul pa sku'i dkyil 'khor bkod de/ shar du badz+ra he ru ka thugs las sprul te bzhugs/ lhor gshin rje gshed po
3b3(1): sku las sprul te bzhugs/ nub tu rta mgrin dbang chen gsung las sprul te bzhugs/ byang du rdo rje gzhon nu phrin las las sprul te bzhugs/ shar lhor gzi brjid las sprul bla med he ru ka bzhugs/ nub byang du
3b4(1): 'jigs byed las sbrul dpal dregs pa kun 'dul bzhugs/ byang shar du stobs las sprul pa stobs ldan nag po bzhugs// lho nub tu rigs pa las sprul pa'i sku/ rig 'dzin rdo rje chos bzhugs su
3b5(1): gsol// de dag la yang so so'i sprul pa yang sbrul sum sbrul khro bo dang / khro mo dang bcas te/ pho brang dgu la gar dgu dang ldan pas khams gsum 'jigs byed dpal gyi chas yongs su rdzogs par yab yum gyi
3b6(1): mkha' gsang las sprul te/ nyid las mi gzhan pa'i 'khor ye shes rang snang gi lha tshogs dang bcas pa rnams dang lhan cig tu 'khod do// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal po las/ gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang
4a1(1): po'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po che mchog he ru ka la/ 'khor rigs bzhi'i he ru ka la sogs pa khro bo dang khro mo rnams dang / gsang ba'i bdag po rdo rje chos
4a2(1): kyis phyag dang bskor ba mdzad de/ mgrin gcig tu 'di skad bstod de zhus pa/ e ma ho// chos dbyings spros bral nam mkha'i thugs klong nas// byams pa'i sprin 'phel zhi dang khro gar mdzad// phrin las yongs
4a3(1): rdzogs char gyis 'gro ba 'dul// phyag 'tshal sangs rgyas kun gyi yang rje la'o// e ma gsang bdag dpal chen he ru ka/ 'gro ba'i dug gzhom yang dag lam gzud phyir// bde gshegs yongs rdzogs dpal
4a4(1): chen thugs gsang ba/ kun 'dus shin tu rnal 'byor rgyud chen stsol// zhes bstod de glus bskul cing gsol ba btab pa las yab kyi dpal chen che mchog he ru kas// rdo rje'i gad rgyangs bsgrags te stsol pa/
4a5(1): kye ho// nyon cig sras mchog rigs 'dus he ru ka/ yab yum 'khor bcas legs par nyon// mun la nyi bzhin dug sel ba// gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud chen bshad// mdor na chos sgo bsam yas kun// 'di
4a6(1): ru 'dus phyir dngos po bcu// bstan rim theg pa'i rnam gzhag dang // lha sgom spyod pa 'bras bu dang // bsnyen dang bsgrub pa chen po dang // dbang bskur dam tshig mtha' rgyas su// rgyud rnams kun gyi gsang ba
4b1(1): 'dus// skal ldan 'khor la longs rdzogs bstan// zhes bka' stsal to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgud kyi rgyal po las/ gnang ba'i skabs phye ba gleng blang ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas
4b2(1): 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams thams cad mgrin gcig tu ston pa kun tu bzang po dpal che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa/ kye kye thams cad ston pa kun tu bzang // dpal chen che mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don bstan pa'i
4b3(1): rnam gzhag de// bdag cag 'khor la bka' stsol cig/ de skad ces ni gsol pa dang // ston pa nyid kyis bka' stsal pa// kye ho 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams rtse gcig nyon// rgyud don bstan pa'i rnam gzhag
4b4(1): bshad// thog mar kun gzhi bcos bslad med// cir yang rgya chad phyogs lhung bral// stong khyab nam mkha' lta bu la// rang rtsal 'gyu byed rlung gis g.yos// ma rig rtog pa'i gzung 'dzin gyis// nan gyis
4b5(1): mkha' la mdud pa bor// rtsal la rang dbang ma thob pas// 'grus dran zin dang chags dbang gis// khams gsum 'khor cing rgyud drug 'khyams// ma rtogs log par rtogs pa las// rtsal la dbang thob kun
4b6(1): bzang gis// grol thabs theg pa sna tshogs bstan// bstan theg pa rim dgu ste// nyan thos rang rgyal byang sems gsum// gang zag dbang po dman la dgongs// kri ya yo ga yu ba gsum// gang zag dbang po
5a1(1): 'bring la dgongs// bskyed dang rdzogs pa a ti gsum// gang zag dbang po rab la dgongs// dbye na dbang po rim dgus ched// re re la yang ngo bo dang // nges tshig dbye ba rang 'dod
5a2(1): kyis// 'jug sgo lta spyod sgom pa dang // phrin las 'bras bu'i rim pa bstan// rgyal dgongs theg pa sna tshogs kyang // gong ma gong ma'i lta ba yis// 'og ma 'og ma rnams la gnod// de phyir rim gyis gong ma
5a3(1): 'phags// theg pa gsum gyi nges 'byung la// theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas// de la 'khor 'das yongs rdzogs pas// mthar thug rnal 'byor nges pa'i don// mngon sum rjes rig tshad du dag/ yi ge/
5a4(1): gsum gyis mngon sangs rgyas// de phyir yongs rdzogs rgyud chen 'dir// rgyud lung man ngag yongs su rdzogs// thun mong ma yin thugs kyi rgyud// 'di las gsang ba'i nges don med// ces bka' stsal
5a5(1): to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal po las/ bstan pa'i rim pa theg pa'i rnam gzhag bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas yang 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams kyis/ ston pa kun tu bzang po
5a6(1): dpal che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa/ kye kye kye/ yang dag don ston kun tu bzang // bla med che mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don lta ba'i rgyal po de// bdag cag rnams la bka' stsal zhu// de skad gsol pa thugs
5b1(1): dgongs te// ston pa chen pos bka' stsal pa// 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs rtse gcig nyon// rgyud don lta ba'i rgyal po ni// gzhi rtsa med pa'i sems nyid 'di// chos rnams kun gyi rtsa ba yin// 'khor dang mya ngan
5b2(1): 'das pa'i chos// ye nas ma bcos chos kyi sku// dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi// thugs dgongs lta ba mthar thug pa// snang srid gzhir bzhengs lta ba ru// 'khor 'das gnyis med yongs su
5b3(1): rdzogs// he ru ka las gzhan ma yin// thig le snying po byang sems brdal// yang dag don gyi gnas lugs te// spros bral thig le gcig tu rdzogs// rang byung rang shar rang grol bas// rang bzhin ma bcos
5b4(1): spros bral bzhag/ khyung chen nam mkhar lding ba bzhin// snang srid spyi rgya rlabs kyis chod// sems las kun 'byung bde gshegs sems// rang las sangs rgyas gzhan na med// bltas pas dpal chen zhal ma
5b5(1): mthong // tshig mtshon dper bya kun las 'das// brjod dang brjod bral gnyis su med// blta bya ma 'gags lta byed med// gnyis med don rtogs chos kyi sku// rang rig sems la sems kyis ltos// ngos
5b6(1): bzung ma grub ngo bos stong // stong pa nyid de rang gsal la// gsal ba'i dus na dngos po med// dngos med de nyid gsal bar shar// de phyir gsal stong gnyis su med// sa le hrig gi 'dzin zhen med// de la
6a1(1): dgongs pa yongs rdzogs te// kun gyis ma rtogs gsang ba dag/ rang la 'dus phyir gsang ba 'dus// theg pa kun gyi rgyal po yin// zhes bka' stsal to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal
6a2(1): po las/ lta ba bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas yang 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams kyis// ston pa kun tu bzang po dpal che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa/ kye kye kye/ rang bzhin ma bcos kun tu
6a3(1): bzang // 'gyur med che mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don bsgom pa'i rgyal po de// bdag cag rnams la bka' stsal zhu// de skad gsol pa thugs dgongs te// ston pa chen pos bka' stsal pa// 'dus pa'i 'khor
6a4(1): tshogs rtse gcig nyon// rgyud don bsgom pa'i rgyal po ni// mi bsgom bsgom don de shes nas// sgo gsum ma bcos sor 'jog pa// bde gshegs yongs rdzogs bsgom pa yin// gdod nas chos sku rang gi
6a5(1): sems// lta bas stong gsal dbyer med rtogs// gdeng 'og chud nas rgyun du gsal// de ni dpal chen bsgom pa yin// byabs kyis chod pa'i lta ba yis// snang srid dpal chen skyu ru bsgom// gsal stong
6a6(1): gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ sgra ru grag tshad ngo bos stong // grag stong gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ yin ni 'gyu dran ngo bos stong // dran stong gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ dbyings dang ye shes gnyis
6b1(1): med cing // thabs shes gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ sangs rgyas sems can gnyis med cing // 'khor 'das gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ yul dang dbang po gnyis med cing // bde sdug gnyis med
6b2(1): bsgom pa'i mchog/ rang rig dpal dang gnyis med cing // lta spyod gnyis med bsgom pa'i mchog/ rnam rtog chos sku gnyis med cing // mtshan ma zil gnon bsgom pa'i mchog/ gnyis med don la dbang thob
6b3(1): na// ting 'dzin yongs rdzogs bsgom pa yin// zhes bka' stsal to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal po las/ bsgom pa bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas yang 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams
6b4(1): kyis// ston pa kun tu bzang po dpal che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa/ kye kye kye/ rang byung rig pa kun tu bzang // bde spyod che mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don spyod pa'i rgyal po ni// bdag cag rnams la bka' stsal
6b5(1): zhu// de skad gsol pa thugs dgongs te// ston pa chen pos bka' stsal pa// 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs rtse gcig nyon// rgyud don spyod pa'i rgyal po ni// gang ltar lta sgom dbyer med pa'i// ngang las 'bral
6b6(1): med spyod pa'i mchog/ nyin snang rtogs pa'i don bstan nas// rmi lam bde ba spyod pa'i mchog/ rigs pa gar 'grus lta ba dran// rang snang 'dzin med spyod pa'i mchog/ 'dzin pa grol bas snang ba dag/ snang ba
7a1(1): yan thub spyod pa'i mchog/ tshogs drug yul zhen rtsad chod nas// 'khor ba rgyas thebs spyod pa'i mchog/ nyams len goms pas rnam rtogs yal// dus bzhi mnyam sbyor spyod pa'i mchog/ mnyam
7a2(1): rjes rtog langs dus gsum du// chos skur grol ba spyod pa'i mchog/ 'khor 'das spang blang rang grol nas// dus gsum bde gshegs spyod pa'i mchog/ snang grag dran rtog thams cad kun// dpal chen sku
7a3(1): gsung thugs spyod pa// rgyal ba yongs rdzogs spyod pa yin// zhes bka' stsal to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal po las/ spyod pa bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas 'dus pa'i 'khor
7a4(1): rnams kyis// dpal kun tu bzang po che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa// kye kye kye/ sku gsum yongs rdzogs kun tu bzang // bdag nyid che mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don 'bras bu'i rgyal po de// bdag cag rnams la
7a5(1): bka' stsal zhu// de skad gsol pa thugs dgongs te// ston pa chen pos bka' stsal pa// 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams rtse gcig nyon// rgyud don 'bras bu'i rgyal po ni// lta ba mngon gyur sgrib g.yogs bral// kun
7a6(1): bzang rgyal po'i 'bras bu yin// smin grol mthar phyir mi bzlog/ dus gsum bde gshegs 'bras bu yin// sangs rgyas bde chen kun 'dus pa// lta ba yongs rdzogs 'bras bu yin// yongs su rdzogs don de
7b1(1): spros dang bral// skye med chos sku'i 'bras bu yin// thugs rje 'gag med zhi khror shar// bde chen longs sku'i 'bras bu yin// gnyis med ngang nas cir yang sprul// 'gro 'dul sbrul sku'i 'bras bu yin// rtogs
7b2(1): na bcos med snying po'i don// ye nas rang snang 'bras bu yin// snang dang mi snang gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu yin// bcos dang ma bcos gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu
7b3(1): yin// lha sgom spyod 'bras gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu yin// phyogs lhung ma lhung gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu yin// rgya chad ma chad gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras
7b4(1): bu yin// dbu ma mtha' ma gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu yin// rang byung gzhan byung gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer med 'bras bu yin// 'khor dang myang 'das gnyis su med// tha dad dbyer
7b5(1): med 'bras bu yin// mthar phyin sku dang ye shes tshogs// thams cad yongs rdzogs 'khrul pa med// he ru ka yi 'bras bu yin// zhes bka' stsal to// dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud kyi rgyal po las/ 'bras bu
7b6(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // de nas yang 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams kyis/ ston pa kun tu bzang po dpal che mchog he ru ka la gsol pa/ kye kye kye/ dkyil 'khor bdag nyid kun tu
8a1(1): bzang // lhag pa'i lha mchog he ru ka/ rgyud don yongs rdzogs lha bsnyen sgrub// bdag cag rnams la bka' stsal zhu// de skad gsol pa thugs dgongs te// ston pa chen pos bka' stsal
8a2(1): pa// 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams rtse gcig nyon// zhi khro yongs rdzogs bsnyen sgrub ni// gzhal yas khang rten sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs// thogs mtha' spros bcad bsgrub lugs mos blor sbyang // chos sku skye ba
8a3(1): med pa'i rang bzhin las// longs sku skye ba'i cho 'phrul gzhal yas lha// zhi khro bde gshegs sbrul sku bsam mi khyab// bde gshegs mkhar mnyam yongs rdzogs rtsa ba'i lha// bcom ldan dpal chen spyi mes
8a4(1): gtsug gi rgyan// thabs shes zung 'jug sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor bas// sbyang gzhi sbyong byed bde chen g.yung drung lha// rigs brgya zhe gnyis lnga gsum yongs rdzogs sku// chags can 'dul phyir thabs gsang rang
8a5(1): byung ba// 'byung bzhi dbang chen gzhal yas 'khyil ba'i dbus// rin chen 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rtsibs bzhi pa// gru chad glo 'bur bar khyams rim par brtsegs// sgo khyud ka brgyad rta babs rgyan sogs
8a6(1): mdzes// a dkar gsal 'tsher zhi ba'i rten mthar thug/ seng ge glang chen rta dang rma bya khyung // rin chen khri rkang pad sdong bar du 'khyil// pad+ma zla ba nyi ma'i gdan steng gsal// mi bskyod mthing ga rdo rje dril bu
8b1(1): 'dzin// snang mdzad dkar po 'khor lo dril bu 'dzin// rin 'byung ser po nor bu dril bu 'dzin// mtha' yas dmar po pad+ma dril bu 'dzin// don grub ljang gu rgya gram dril bu 'dzin// kun kyang rdzogs skyil
8b2(1): gnyis med yum chen ni// bzang mo spyan dang mA ma gos dkar sgrol// g.yas pa rigs 'dzin g.yon dri la yab la 'khyud// kun bzang yid mthing rdo rje dril bu bsnams// bzang mo chos mthing mnyam gzhag phyag
8b3(1): rgya gsal// sbrul 'khor sa snying nam mkha'i snying po dang // spyan ras gzigs dbang phyag na rdo rje ming // lA s+ye mA le gIrti ni rti sring // kun bzang byams pa sgrib sel 'jam dbyangs ming // me tog bdud spros
8b4(1): mar me dri chab sring // lha dbang zags bzang sha ka thub ser rab brtan// kha 'bar chos rgyal la sogs thub pa drug/ gshin rje stobs chen rta mgrin bdud rtsi 'khyil// ro langs mi 'pham ral gcig khro gnyer
8b5(1): yum// 'khor rnams nyi ma'i zer ltar rang bzhin 'du// rin chen rgyan rdzogs tshul dgu'i gar ldan mdzes// de las spro bsdu cho 'phrul cir yang bde/ bde chen longs spyod rdzogs sku kun gyi rgyal// bsam gyis
8b6(1): mi khyab bder 'dus rigs brgya yongs// rtsa ba lngar rdzogs de nyid kun rdzogs pa// gcig dang tha da stong nyid snying rje bstan// bdag nyid rdo rje sems dpa' shel gyi mdog/ rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs zhal
9a1(1): gcig phyag gnyis pa// phyag g.yas rdo rje rtse lnga thugs kar bsnams// g.yon pas dngul dkar dril bu dku la brten// zhabs gnyis skyil krung nyi zla pad dkyil bzhugs// zhi tshul rgyan chas 'od
9a2(1): zer sna tshogs 'bar// dung khang 'khor lo ljags pad thugs rdo rje// oM dkar AHdmar hUM mthing 'phro 'dur bzlas// gyen du bde gshegs sku gsung thugs mchod bskul// thur du snod bcud lus ngag yid
9a3(1): sgrib sbyang // tshur 'dus sku gsung thugs bcud dngos grub bsdu// rang sems rnam dag rdo rje sems dpa' yis// sku gsung thugs su bde bar gshegs par bstan// rgyud lung man ngag yongs rdzogs sgo nas
9a4(1): bsgrub// dgra gsum bdud bzhi 'gro drug g.yang sa bcad// sum cu phrag drug gis 'grub las rnams 'grub// sku dang ye shes yongs rdzogs lhun gyis grub// rang bzhin zhi ba'i dkyil 'khor rnam bkod
9a5(1): la// bde gshegs rgyal ba yongs gyis dbu rgyan no// de ltar phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba yongs rdzogs rnams// gdug pa 'dul phyir khro bo rol par bstan// rab tu gdul dka' khro zhing gtum pa la// zhi des lkug
9a6(1): pas phan par mi 'gyur phyir// zhi tshogs dbu yi gtsug tu rab bsdus nas// bcom ldan de gshegs rgyal ba yongs rdzogs pa// rab 'jigs khro bo rol pa'i dkyil 'khor bstan// stong gsal rgyu las rang
9b1(1): byung gzhal yas ni// chos dbyings mi 'gyur mthing nag gru gsum e// stobs chen g.yo byed ljang nag kha gdengs yaM// thugs rje'i rlan gyis kun sdud dmar nag ra// rab brtan kun shong bcu gsum rdzogs
9b2(1): byed suM// 'od gsal smin byed dngos 'joms dmar ser raM// rdo rje sra mkhregs rus pa'i ri rab stengs// phyi dang nang gsal rin chen yongs rdzogs b+h+rUM// gzhal yas bkod pa tshad med rnam dag dbus// theg
9b3(1): pa dgu rdzogs dpal chen dkyil 'khor dgu// 'khor 'das dbyer med ye shes sgo dgur gsal// ye shes lnga rdzogs rtsibs bzhi lte bar bcas// thugs rje'i zer ldan spros bral mu khyud mdzes// yon tan ma
9b4(1): bkag rin chen zur brgyad ldan// mtshan nyid bzhi rdzogs gru chad rnam bzhis spras// de bzhin pho brang dgu la phrin las rdzogs// bdud 'joms ka bzhi chu srin gdan stengs btsugs// thabs shes nyi zla'i ka
9b5(1): zhus zhing gdung btegs// thugs rjes gdal khyab rA tra'i lpags thog phub// sku gsum lhun grub thod tshar sum brtsegs la// gnam lcags rig rtsal gzer gyis rab tu bsdams// ye shes bzhi ldan zang thal
9b6(1): nang sgo bzhi// ye shes zer lngas gling dgu'i bar mtshams bres// chags pa'i thugs rjes rak+ta'i zham chu 'bab// snying po'i don rtogs tsit+ta'i pho ltos brgyan// chos sku mnyam rdzogs par khyams 'khor yug
10a1(1): brdal// dgos 'dod re skong rin chen sna lngas brtsigs// tshad med bzhi ldan sgo bzhi phyogs bzhir bgrad// rnam thar brgyad kyi them skas rim par brtan// thugs rjes 'dzin phyir chu srin ya them
10a2(1): mdzes// 'byung po sri 'dul ma them rus sbal brjid// gdug pa tshar gcod sbrul nag skyes bu btsugs// 'khor ba rgyun gcod zhing lpags sgo logs bcad// chos kyi gaN+DI cong dang dril bu bsgrags// yul
10a3(1): brgyad 'dzin bcom klu brgyad ka gdan stengs// tshogs brgyad rang dag lha brgyad ka bar btsugs// thabs shes brgyad ldan gza' brgyad ka zhur bskal// bcu drug rol pa'i zhing spug gdung chen bkram// 'gru
10a4(1): byed rang 'grol kun grol rgyu skar dral grab bkram// bzang ngan med mnyam zhing chen lpags thog bkram// ma rig mun sel nyi zla'i skar khung mdzes// 'khor 'das spyi chings chos sku'i bre bum pa// skyon gyis ma
10a5(1): gos bum stan pad+mar gsal// sa lam yongs rdzogs 'khor 'degs 'khor lo brtsegs// kun khyab theg pa'i yongs rtser gdugs tog rngam// bstan pa'i spyi phud bya ru dar dpyangs brgyan// phrin las bzhi
10a6(1): rdzogs rat+na'i rta babs brtsegs// chags bral pad stengs chos 'khor rab tu mdzes// rgya chad phyos su ma lhung zhing gdugs phub// rang byung mi nub mi mgo'i rin chen tog/ rig stong dbyer med ri dwags chu srin
10b1(1): mdzes// dbyings rig yongs 'brel sprin nag grib so gtibs// dbyings las rtsal shar sgo khang rgyan dgus mdzes// 'dod yon zhen med spyod phyir 'dod khyams bskor// dbyings nas kun snang mu tig thod
10b2(1): ras spras// ma 'dres yongs rdzogs shel gyi mchod rten dkrigs// sna tshogs 'od gsal mchog phran da ru ka/ ma rig sgrib sel bcu gcig rdo rje gseng // thabs kyis sgrib sel zla phyed rdo rjes brgyan// bdud
10b3(1): 'joms zhing drang lha chen rgyal mtshan brgyad// 'khor ba'i g.yul rgyal zhing chen 'phan brgyad phyar// don rtags brgyad ldan dur khrod brgyad kyis bskor// tshul bcu'i mtha' grol he ru'i gnas bcus
10b4(1): gtams// khams gsum zil gnon rgya gram rwa bzhis mnan// ma chags phrin las kun khyab pad stong brdal// sangs rgyas stong rdzogs 'khor lo rtsibs stong phrab// gsang sngags snying po 'gyur med brag ris
10b5(1): gtams// gnyen pos mi shigs rdo rje'i ra bas bskor// gzung 'dzin nags sreg ye shes me lnga 'bar// byol song dregs pa nyi zla pad gdan brjid// dgos 'dod kun 'byung gter bum dpag bsam
10b6(1): rgyas// snang srid yongs rdzogs gzhal yas khang chen gsal// phyi nang 'khor lo rin chen gsang ba e// zhi khro'i rgyan sogs dbye'am yongs rdzogs pa// gang la gang 'dul dkyil 'khor 'phrul shes bya// gzhal
11a1(1): yas de dag rnal 'byor rang lus la// yongs rdzogs sgrub rten mchod rdzas dur khrod rdzogs// de yang rang rig sems kyi dkyil 'khor du// yongs rdzogs thig le nyag gcig ngo mtshar te// rgya chad
11a2(1): phyogs lhung kun bral gzhal mtha' yas// dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kun gyi mthar zug yin// sgrub rdzas rten gyi rim pa mchod bcas ni// sku gsung thugs yon phrin las dmigs pa'i rten// sku rten
11a3(1): gzugs la gsung rten snying po dgod// yon tan bdud rtsi phrin las phur pa bsham// sgos rten zhi ba mthar thug a dkar la// che mchog yongs rdzogs sgrub rten bum mthar thug/ de bzhin yang dag me gcig/
11a4(1): gshin rje phram// pad+ma rta thod rta zhal phrin phur gcig/ ma mo nal snying rig 'dzin sku gcig ma// dregs pa sku gcig drag sngags byang gcig ste// rten rnams yongs rdzogs sgrub rdzas rang lus yin// rig pa'i
11a5(1): sems nyid sgrub rten kun mthar thug/ 'dod yon rdzas 'jom phyi yi mchod pas te// rang lus rang byung bdud rtsi nang mchod rdzas// rtog tshogs rang byung rang grol gsang mchod de// yid chos dbyer med ngang
11a6(1): dwadangs mchod mthar thug/ dkyil 'khor lte dbus zla kham e yi dkyil// chos dbyings a las rang byung lhun grub lha// kun bzang che mchog khro rgyal he ru ka/ mthing nag zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi
11b1(1): bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing bzhad gshe rngam// g.yas gsum rtse dgu rtse lnga rtse gsum bsnams// g.yon gsum b+han+da dung dmar thod khrag bsnams// rdo rje'i gsheg g.yas rin chen gshog
11b2(1): g.yon gdengs// sku gsung thugs ldan srog gi ye shes gsal// dpal gyi chas bcu dur khrod rgyan yongs spras// zhabs bzhi dor stabs g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskums tshul// gnam zhal yum chen zhal
11b3(1): gcig phyag gnyis mthing // phyag g.yas rtse gsum gtsor khyud g.yon dmar stob// zhabs g.yas yab 'khril g.yon brkyang gtso la sbyor// rigs lngas dbu rgyan dur khrod rgyan drug gsol// gnyis med rab
11b4(1): 'jigs me dpung klong na brjid// brdas bskul mkha' gsang rab sbyor sbrul sras 'gyed// shar gyi rtsibs stengs rak+Sha he ru ka/ smug nag zhal gcig phyag gnyis 'khor lo g.yas// g.yon pa zod khrag zhabs
11b5(1): nyis brkyang bskum 'gyings// rak+Sha kro ti shwa rI cha lugs yab 'dra 'khril// lho rtsibs g+ha ya he ru ka ser nag/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis rin chen thod khrag bsnams// g+hA ya kro ti shwa rI yab 'dra 'khril// nub
11b6(1): rtsibs bi shwa he ru ka dmar nag/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis pad+ma thod khrag bsnams// bi shra kro d+hi shwa rI yab 'dra 'khril// byang rtsibs yak+Sha he ru ka ljang nag/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis rgya gram thod
12a1(1): khrag thogs// yak+Sha kro d+hi shwa rI yab 'dra 'khril// dur khrod chas gsol brda rtags gtso dang 'dra// nyi dang zer bzhin sprul pa'i 'khor tshogs ni// phyogs skyong dregs 'dul khro bo chen po bcu// ta
12a2(1): kr-ita sgo skyong pho nya bstan srung bcas// che mchog yon tan yongs rdzogs rang byung shar// phyogs mtshams pho brang brgyad du thugs kyi sras// dkyil 'khor shar dbus zla kham e yi dkyil// ru dra nyi zla pad+ma 'od
12a3(1): 'bar steng // bcom ldan thugs mchog badz+ra he ru ka/ mthing nag zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing bzhad rngam gshe// g.yas gsum rdo rje kha T+wAM rnge chung
12a4(1): bsnams// g.yon gsum dril bu b+han dmar rgyu zhags bsnams// gshog gnyis zhabs bzhi brkyangs bskums dor stabs tshul// sku gsung thugs srog dur khrod chas rnams rdzogs// kro d+hI shwa rI yum chen sku la
12a5(1): 'khril// phyag zhabs chas sogs brdas bskul gtso dang 'dra// shar gyi rtsibs stengs bud+d+ha he ru ka/ smug nag g.yas pa rdo rje g.yon rgyu zhags/ bud+d+ha kro d+hi g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// lho yi rtsibs steng rat+na
12a6(1): he ru ka/ ser nag g.yas g.yon rat+na stong gsum bsnams// rat+na kro ti g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// nub tu rtsibs steng pad+ma he hu ka/ dmar nag g.yas pa pad+ma ti ra bsnams// pad+ma kro d+hI g.yas 'khyud
12b1(1): g.yon dmar stob// byang gi rtsibs stengs karma he ru ka/ ljang nag g.yas g.yon rgya gram ri rab bsnams// karma kro d+hi g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// sbrul 'khor ko ri ma brgyad sid+ha brgyad// sgo skyong bka'
12b2(1): srung yang dag thugs rdzogs shar// dkyil 'khor lho dbus zla kham e yi dkyil// chu glang nyi zla pad+ma 'od 'bar steng // bcom ldan sku mchog 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed// mthing nag zhal gsum phyag drug
12b3(1): zhabs bzhi bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing bzhad gshe rngam// g.yas gsum 'khor lo ral gri dgra sta bsdams// g.yon gsum sdig mdzub mdung dang b+han dmar bsnams// gshog gnyis
12b4(1): zhabs bzhi brkyangs bskums dor stabs bgrad// sku gsung thugs srog dur khrod chas rnams rdzogs// sbyor yum be tA lI ni sku la 'khril// sgrol yum tsa tI tri shUl b+han dmar bsnams// phyag zhabs chas rdzogs
12b5(1): brdas bskul gtso dang 'dra// shar rtsibs gsod byed ya ma rA dza mthing // g.yas pa 'khor lo g.yon pa dgra sta bsnams// nag mo ral gcig g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// lho rtsibs myos byed 'bar ba
12b6(1): ser nag la// g.yas pa be con g.yon pa dgra sta bsnams// gtum mo dug hrul g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// nub rtsibs Ar+ya me ru tse dmar po// g.yas pa dung khrag g.yon pa dbyug to bsnams// 'od
13a1(1): zer can ma g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob/ byang rtsibs ral pa tshar dgu ldang nag la// g.yas pa gtun shing g.yon pa dung dmar bsnams// nag mo re ti g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar
13a2(1): stob// sbrul 'khor phyogs skyong chen po bcu gnyis dang // sgo skyong bka' srung 'jam dpal sku rdzogs shar// dkyil 'khor nub dbus zla gam e yi dkyil// klu brgyad nyi zla pad+ma 'od 'bar steng // bcom ldan
13a3(1): gsung mchog pad+ma dbang chen sku// dmar nag zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon sngo dbus dmar bzhad gshe rngam// g.yas gsum rdo rje kha T+wAM sbrul zhags bsnams// g.yon gsum
13a4(1): dril chen b+han dmar lcags sgrog bsnams// gshog gnyis zhabs bzhi brkyangs bskums dor stabs tshul// sku gsung thugs srog dur khrod chas kun rdzogs// pad+ma gzi ldan bde chen yum mchog 'khril// phyag
13a5(1): zhabs chas rdzogs brdas bskul gtso dang 'dra// shar rtsibs steng du rdo rje dbang chen dkar// g.yas pa rdo rje g.yon pa zod khrag bsnams// rdo rje dbang phyug g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// lho rtsibs steng du
13a6(1): rin chen dbang chen ser// g.yas pa rin chen g.yon pa thod khrag bsnams// rat+na dbang phyug g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// nub rtsibs steng du pad+ma dbang chen dmar// g.yas pa pad dkar g.yon pa thod

13b2(1): stob// sbrul 'khor zil gnon khro bo yab yum brgyad// sgo skyong bka' srung pad+ma gsung rdzogs shar// dkyil 'khor byang dbus zla gam e yi dbus// lha chen nyi zla pad+ma 'od 'bar stengs// bcom ldan las
13b3(1): chog rdo rje gzhon nu'i sku// mthing nag zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing bzhad gshe rngam// g.yas g.yon dang po rtse dgu me dpung bsnams// bar gnyis rtse
13b4(1): lnga kha T+wAM mthar phur 'dril// gshog gnyis zhabs bzhi brkyangs bskums dor stabs tshul// sku gsung thugs srog dur khrod chas rnams rdzogs// 'khor lo rgyab 'debs yum chen sku la 'khril// phyag zhabs
13b5(1): chas sogs brdas bskul gtso dang 'dra// shar rtsibs sras mchog bud+d+ha kI la dkar// g.yas pa phur pa g.yon pa thod khrag bsnams// yum gcig sangs rgyas g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// lho rtsibs sras
13b6(1): mchog rat+na kI la ser// g.yas pa dgra sta g.yon pa thod khrag bsnams// yum chen rin chen g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// nub rtsibs sras mchog pad+ma kI la dmar// g.yas pa gri gug g.yon pa thod khrag
14a1(1): bsnams// yum gcig pad+ma g.yas 'khyud g.yon dmar stob// byang rtsibs sras mchog karma kI la ldang // g.yas pa mdung thung g.yon pa thod khrag bsnams// yum gcig las byed g.yas 'khyud
14a2(1): g.yon dmar stob// sbrul 'khor khro bcu yab yum za gsod bcas// sgo skyong bka' srung phrin las phur tshogs shar// shar lho'i dkyil 'khor zla gam e dbus su// ma mo nyi zla pad+ma 'od 'bar steng // dpal
14a3(1): chen bla med gsang ba mngon rdzogs sku// mthing nag zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing brjid dang ldan// g.yas gsum rdo rje khyung khra sbrul zhags

14a5(1): rdzogs// 'khor lo'i rtsibs shar rnam snang gsal dkar mo// zhal gcig phyag gnyis rdo rje thod khrag bsnams// 'khor lo'i lho rtsibs 'od gsal 'bar ser mo// zhal gcig phyag gnyis rin chen thod khrag
14a6(1): bsnams// 'khor lo'i nub rtsibs gnyen gsal 'bar dmar mo// zhal gcig phyag gnyis pad+ma thod khrag bsnams// 'khor lo'i byang rtsibs yang gsal g.yas sngon mo// zhal gcig phyag gnyis rgya gram thod
14b1(1): khrag bsnams// dpal chen mdun zur bkrag gsal mnyam mthing nag/ zhal gcig phyag gnyis 'khor lo thod khrag bsnams// sbrul 'khor rje mo sman mo bdun chu gnyis// sgo skyong bka' srung rbod gtong
14b2(1): yongs rdzogs shar// lho nub dkyil 'khor zla gam e yi dbus// seng chen dar gyi pho long pad brtsegs steng // dpal chen rdo rje thod pa rtsal mchog sku// zhal phyag sku mdog phyag mtshan sna tshogs kyang // mi

14b4(1): ldem pa dar dmar bcings// 'khor lo'i rtsibs shar lhun grub rig 'dzin dkar// rtsibs lhor phyag rgya chen po'i rig 'dzin ser// nub rtsibs tshe la dbang ba'i rig 'dzin dmar// byang rtsibs rnam par smin
14b5(1): 'i rig 'dzin ljang // kun kyang zhal gcig phyag gnyis thor tshugs can// rin chen rus pa dar sna'i rgyan gyis spras// sbrul 'khor grub pa'i rig 'dzin chen po brgyad// sgo skyong bka' srung rig 'dzin yongs

15a1(1): bgrad// g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus mthing rngam la 'jigs// g.yas gsum rdo rje lha brgyad mgo bo 'dzin// g.yon gsum b+han dmar klu brgyad mgo bo bsnams// srid pa spyi 'dul sku la
15a2(1): dgyes par 'khril// 'khor rtsibs shar du ya ma rA dza nag/ g.yas pa be con g.yon pa thod dbyug bsnams// sgrol byed yum nag 'khor lo thod khrag stob// 'khor rtsibs lho ru skos rje drang dkar nag/ g.yas
15a3(1): pa khram shing g.yon pa thod khrag bsnams// nag mo re ti khram shing nad rgyal thogs// 'khor rtsibs nub tu srin po glog phreng nag/ g.yas pa glog phreng g.yon pa ser ba thogs// sbal mgo khrag mig phur pa mi
15a4(1): mgo 'dzin// 'khor rtsibs byang du gnod sprin me dpal nag/ g.yas pa rin chen g.yon pa zangs gri bsnams// gnod sbyin sngon mo spu gri g.yu sbrang thogs// sbrul 'khor sde dpon nyi shu rab 'jigs
15a5(1): bskor// yang sbrul mgo sbyong 'jig rten dregs tshogs shar// byang shar dkyil 'khor zla gam e yi dbus// dgra bgegs nyi zla pad+ma 'bar ba'i steng // dpal chen drag po stobs ldan nag po'i sku// zhal gsum
15a6(1): phyag drug zhabs bzhi dor stabs bgrad// dbu gsum mthing nag nag dang nag 'tsher khros// g.yas gsum rdo rje lha brgyad tsit+ta bsnams// g.yon gsum thod khrag klu brgyad tsit+ta 'dzin// 'byung lnga'i bdag mo
15b1(1): gzugs 'degs 'dod khams gnon// rtsibs shar gshin rje 'chi bdag nag po'i sgra// g.yas pa gri gug g.yon pa zod khrag bsnams// gsod byed nag mo zangs gri tsiSh+Tha 'dzin// rtsibs lhor bdud nag me
15b2(1): yi kha rlangs can// g.yas pa kha T+wAM g.yon pa tri shUl thogs// bdud ma nag mo khram shing thod rlon 'dzin// nub rtsibs srin po gsod byed 'bar ba smug/ g.yas pa ral gri g.yon pa thod khrag thogs// za byed
15b3(1): nag mo gri gug thod khrag thogs// byang rtsibs gnod sbyin gang ba bzang po sngo// g.yas pa ral gri g.yon pa dar nag 'phyar// sha za sngon mo dar nag mi lpags thogs// sbrul 'khor sde dpon 'jigs byed bcu
15b4(1): yis bskor// sngags bdag dregs pa yongs rdzogs drag po shar// kun kyang khro rngam sgeg pa dpa' la 'jigs// snying rje'i spyan ldan gar dgu'i chas rdzogs gsal// dkyil 'khor chen po'i phyi khyams 'khor
15b5(1): yug tu// sbrul 'khor yang sbrul bka' nyan pho nya ste// sbrul 'khor gong spros sras min bde brjod rnams// mngon spyod las kyis gdul dka'i 'gro 'dul phyir// sku mdog sna tshogs gdab phur brgya rtsar
15b6(1): gsal// mkha' 'gro ging gtso bzhi bzhi ma sring shar// sgo bzhi skyong mdzad khro rgyal yab yum brgyad// ya mAn+ta kr-ita dkar po thod dbyug lcags kyu thogs// pra dz+nyAn+ta kr-ita ser po rtse gsum zhags pa thogs// pad+man+ta
16a1(1): kr-ita dmar po thod sbrul lcags sgrog thogs// big+h+nAn+ta kr-ita ljang gu rgya gram dril bu thogs// rta gdong dkar mo phag nag spre'u dmar sbyong gdong ldang // lcags kyu zhags pa lcags sgrog dril 'khrol
